Jupiter Devours- Maelynn Le<//name>

1616532900677<//time>
< Rating>
4< /Rating>
< Text>
Amorino Gelato first originated in Europe and has brought their Italian gelato flavors to the US. I had the pleasure of going to Grant Ave. location in San Francisco, CA which is near Chinatown. They are known for their signature gelatos that are shaped in the prettiest flowers you have ever seen topped with a macaron! I got to try their classic size gelato flower with the flavors being pistachio, strawberry, and mango topped with a blueberry cheesecake macaron. They only do take-out only and the place does its very best to follow the COVID safety procedures.

So I got the flavor combination of strawberry, mango, and pistachio. Overall, I chose a really great flavor combination for my gelato. I can really taste the strawberry and mango flavor very well and one flavor does not overtake another flavor. I thought it was really delicious and would really go back for more. I liked the pistachio too however, I wish there were more of the pistachio nuts (yes there were some but not a lot I did taste) to give the pistachio flavor to stand out more and also for texture too. I did taste pistachio however it wasn‚Äôt as dominant as the strawberry and mango flavors. The blueberry cheesecake was perfect to the taste however it was a bit too soft for my liking because when I tried to pick it up, it immediately cracked so be careful with your macarons!

Overall, this place serves really delicious gelato and the staff was super kind to me. I would definitely check this place out when you can because this is the real deal gelato you're witnessing right here!</Text>

Interesting place. Went there with a friend, I got pistachio,  hazelnut, chocolate and straciatella. Chocolate and hazelnut were great, pistachio was ok, flavorwise. What was annoying is the fact that you have to buy first (pay for a cone, cup etc.) before trying out different ice creams. You then tell them what to put into your cone/cup. While they tell you that they will refund you if you don't want anything, it is clear that they are betting on the fact that people are too lazy to ask for a refund.
Girl at the counter was quite slow, both in terms of working as well as answering our question. Manager seemed annoyed by the fact that we were annoyed that we had to pay first before tasting.

Ice cream: 4/5
Service: 3/5
Business model: 2/5</Text>

<userid>114163658858039149063</userid><Name>Marie T Fisher</Name><time>1514834964897</time><rate>3< /rate>< review>
If you've been spoiled by city Goodwill locations that contain plenty of high-end treasures, you will be disappointed by the Alameda Goodwill. While the staff are friendly, this location is small with limited parking, the quality of merchandise isn't great, and the clothing is all lower quality brands that have been washed/worn extensively. Additionally, and this is a bit weird, the clothing is all priced the same (eg, all shirts are the same price, all pants are the same price, etc). The household goods are also well-used. They do have a bin with used records, and a wall of used books, which may be worth checking out if that's your thing.<//review>

< review>
Beautiful shop!! Friendliest owner and employees!!

While on a mission to find an inexpensive, used mannequin for sale, I happened across IDS while en route to a display store in downtown LA. Intrigued by a window of gorgeous dressmaker forms on display, I went inside to see if they rented or sold mannequins as well. WOW! What a beautiful store! Although I‚Äôm not a person who sews, I could see that anyone who does sew, would appreciate the incredible selection of implements and tools of the trade. The shop is quaint and merchandised with a keen eye for detail; filled with decorative accents throughout and cool rustic finishes. Rosa (the lovely owner!), greeted me and began her search for a form or mannequin in the storage room. In moments, she procured a full mannequin and told me that she didn‚Äôt need it, that it was just taking up space. I was so thrilled! But then the most incredible thing happened - she GAVE me the mannequin!! She didn‚Äôt want anything for it, she just wished it to be used instead of sitting in storage. No one gives things away, ever. This kind act saved my entire month. Thank you again, Rosa!

Rosa Casarez has established herself as an artist and it shows. Do yourself a favor, take a break from online shopping and go visit IDS-LA! You‚Äôll enjoy the ambiance and probably find something to inspire you!<//review>

<rate>3</rate>< text>
The prices of fuel are comparable to the other stations around the area.  Their car wash is both good and bad.  I live in an apartment, and can't wash my car in the conventional way.  I like that it's a touch-less wash (they use pressurized water).  This let me at least knock enough of the heavy dirt and dust off of my car so I could go home and use a water-less wash.  The wash does take a long time, though, so I would skip it if there was a line.< /text>

<rating>5<//rating><response>None</response><GmapID>0x8085b736b01c1829:0x26254531869b92aa< /GmapID>< text>
A wonderful farm created from the awareness that farm animals deserve to live good lives, with dignity - in the open air, under the sun, eating healthy foods - before being slaughtered. Even as a vegetarian, I'm totally in alignment with this philosophy. They offer farm tours at noon on Saturdays and Sundays - a great experience for the kids, and for anyone who wants to know where meat comes from, and to see animals living good, signifies lives.</text>
